#<RarityMatchingItemGlowsV3>

    #<Description>

        By Aaron0000

        Gives the glowy bits on weapons/grenades a change of color to match their rarity. You can have it apply to non-elemental versions only (On by default, applies to weapons only), or all versions.

        Note;

        Gemstone glows override the elemental glows, there isn't a way around this.

        If you're using mods that change the rarity of a weapon, there are overrides that allow you to change the glow to match the rarity of your modded weapon (Unique, Legendary, Pearlescent, Seraph, or the Uniques from my BL1-Style Rarities).

        Examples;

        http://imgur.com/a/4TF9w

    #</Description>

    #<Code>

        #<Item Glows>

            #<Weapons>

                #<No Elemental Glow Override>

                    #<Whites>

                        #<Bandit>

                            #<Pistols>

                                set GD_Weap_Pistol.Body.Pistol_Body_Bandit MaterialVectorParameterValues ((ParameterName="p_EmissiveColor",ParameterValue=(R=2.550000,G=2.550000,B=2.550000,A=1.000000),ExpressionGUID=(A=1475816242,B=1139906328,C=-187360584,D=-1825963319)))

                            #</Pistols>

                            #<Assault Rifles>

                                set GD_Weap_AssaultRifle.Body.AR_Body_Bandit MaterialVectorParameterValues ((ParameterName="p_EmissiveColor",ParameterValue=(R=2.550000,G=2.550000,B=2.550000,A=1.000000),ExpressionGUID=(A=1475816242,B=1139906328,C=-187360584,D=-1825963319)))

                            #</Assault Rifles>

                            #<SMGs>

                                set GD_Weap_SMG.Body.SMG_Body_Bandit MaterialVectorParameterValues ((ParameterName="p_EmissiveColor",ParameterValue=(R=2.550000,G=2.550000,B=2.550000,A=1.000000),ExpressionGUID=(A=1475816242,B=1139906328,C=-187360584,D=-1825963319)))

                            #</SMGs>

                            #<Shotguns>

                                set GD_Weap_Shotgun.Body.SG_Body_Bandit MaterialVectorParameterValues ((ParameterName="p_EmissiveColor",ParameterValue=(R=2.550000,G=2.550000,B=2.550000,A=1.000000),ExpressionGUID=(A=1475816242,B=1139906328,C=-187360584,D=-1825963319)))

                            #</Shotguns>

                            #<Launchers>

                                set GD_Weap_Launchers.Body.L_Body_Bandit MaterialVectorParameterValues ((ParameterName="p_EmissiveColor",ParameterValue=(R=2.550000,G=2.550000,B=2.550000,A=1.000000),ExpressionGUID=(A=1475816242,B=1139906328,C=-187360584,D=-1825963319)))

                            #</Launchers>

                        #</Bandit>
